This Tender Offer Statement on Schedule TO (this
Schedule TO) relates to the offer by Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc., a Florida corporation (the Purchaser) and a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard Data Systems Inc., a Delaware corporation (SunGard), to purchase all
of the outstanding shares of common stock (the Shares) of H.T.E., Inc., a Florida corporation (HTE), at a purchase price of $7.00 per Share, in cash, without interest thereon, upon the terms and subject to the conditions set
forth in the Offer to Purchase, dated February 14, 2003, and in the related Letter of Transmittal, copies of which are filed with this Schedule TO as Exhibits (a)(1) and (a)(2) hereto, respectively. This Schedule TO is being filed on behalf of the
Purchaser and SunGard. The information set forth in the Offer to Purchase, including Schedule I thereto, and the Letter of Transmittal are hereby incorporated by reference in answer to Items 1-9 and 11 of this Schedule TO.

Offer To Purchase



Exhibit (a)(1) 
Offer to Purchase for Cash 

All Outstanding Shares of Common Stock 
of

H.T.E., Inc. 
by 
Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc. 
a wholly owned subsidiary of 

SunGard Data Systems Inc. 
at 
$7.00 Per Share 

THE OFFER AND WITHDRAWAL RIGHTS WILL EXPIRE AT 12:00 MIDNIGHT, 
NEW YORK CITY TIME, ON FRIDAY, MARCH 14, 2003, UNLESS THE OFFER IS 
EXTENDED. 

The
Offer (as defined in this Offer to Purchase) is being made pursuant to an Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated February 4, 2003 (the Merger Agreement), by and among SunGard Data Systems Inc., a Delaware corporation (SunGard),
Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc., a Florida corporation and a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard (the Purchaser), and H.T.E., Inc., a Florida corporation (HTE), pursuant to which, following the purchase by the Purchaser of shares
of HTE common stock, par value $0.01 per share, in the Offer and the satisfaction or waiver of each of the conditions to the Offer set forth in the Merger Agreement, the Purchaser will be merged with and into HTE (the Merger), with HTE
surviving the Merger as a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard. As a result of the Merger, each outstanding share of HTE common stock (other than shares owned by SunGard, the Purchaser, HTE or any wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard or HTE) will be
converted into the right to receive the price per share paid in the Offer in cash, without interest thereon. 

HTEs board of directors has, at a meeting held on February 1, 2003, by the unanimous vote of all directors of HTE, (i) determined
that the Merger Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby, including the Offer and the Merger, are fair to, and in the best interests of, the shareholders of HTE; (ii) adopted and approved the Merger Agreement and approved the transactions
contemplated thereby, including the Offer and the Merger; (iii) declared that the Merger Agreement is advisable; and (iv) resolved to recommend that the shareholders of HTE accept the Offer and tender their shares in the Offer. Accordingly, the HTE
board of directors unanimously recommends that the shareholders of HTE tender their shares of HTE common stock pursuant to the Offer and vote to adopt the Merger Agreement at any meeting of shareholders of HTE that may be called to consider such
adoption. 

The Offer is conditioned upon, among
other things, there being validly tendered in accordance with the terms of the Offer and not properly withdrawn prior to the Expiration Date (as defined in this Offer to Purchase) that number of shares of HTE common stock that, together with the
shares then solely beneficially owned by the Purchaser and SunGard (if any), represent a majority of the number of shares constituting the sum of all then outstanding shares plus all shares issuable upon the exercise of all then outstanding options
(which number of shares is referred to as HTEs Adjusted Outstanding Shares and which condition is referred to as the Minimum Condition). The Offer is also subject to other conditions described in Section 13 (Certain
Conditions to the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase. 

A summary of the principal terms of the Offer appears on pages 1 to 9. You should read this entire document carefully before deciding whether to tender your shares in the Offer. 



IMPORTANT 

Any shareholder of HTE who desires to tender all or any portion of such shareholders shares of HTE
common stock to the Purchaser in the Offer should either (i) complete and sign the Letter of Transmittal (or a facsimile copy of it) for the Offer, which is enclosed with this Offer to Purchase, in accordance with the instructions contained in the
Letter of Transmittal (having such shareholders signature on the Letter of Transmittal guaranteed if required by Instruction 1 to the Letter of Transmittal), mail or deliver the Letter of Transmittal (or a facsimile copy of it) and any other
required documents to the depositary for the Offer, Wells Fargo Bank Minnesota, N.A. (the Depositary), and either deliver the certificates representing such shares to the Depositary along with the Letter of Transmittal (or a facsimile
copy of it) or tender such shares by book-entry transfer by following the procedures described in Section 2 (Procedures for Tendering Shares of HTE Common Stock in the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase, in each case prior to the Expiration Date of
the Offer, or (ii) request such shareholders broker, dealer, bank, trust company or other nominee to effect the transaction for such shareholder. Any shareholder of HTE with shares of HTE common stock registered in the name of a broker,
dealer, bank, trust company or other nominee must contact that institution in order to tender such shares to the Purchaser in the Offer. 

Any shareholder of HTE who desires to tender shares of HTE common stock to the Purchaser in the Offer and whose certificates representing
such shares are not immediately available, or who cannot comply in a timely manner with the procedures for tendering shares by book-entry transfer, or who cannot deliver all required documents to the Depositary prior to the Expiration Date of the
Offer, may tender such shares to the Purchaser in the Offer by following the procedures for guaranteed delivery described in Section 2 (Procedures for Tendering Shares of HTE Common Stock in the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase.

connection with the Offer, may be directed to the Information Agent for the Offer at its address and telephone number set forth below. Additional copies of this Offer to Purchase, the Letter of Transmittal, the Notice of Guaranteed Delivery and
other related materials may be obtained from the Information Agent.

SUMMARY TERM SHEET 

We are Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc., and we are making an offer to purchase all of the outstanding shares of
common stock of H.T.E., Inc. The following are some of the questions you, as a shareholder of HTE, may have about our offer and our answers to those questions. This Summary Term Sheet provides important and material information about our offer that
is described in more detail elsewhere in this Offer to Purchase, but this Summary Term Sheet may not include all of the information about our offer that is important to you. We urge you to carefully read the remainder of this Offer to Purchase and
the Letter of Transmittal for our offer because the information in this Summary Term Sheet is not complete. Additional important information about our offer is contained in the remainder of this Offer to Purchase and the Letter of Transmittal for
our offer. We have included cross-references in this Summary Term Sheet to other Sections of this Offer to Purchase to direct you to the sections of this Offer to Purchase in which a more complete description of the topics covered in this Summary
Term Sheet appear. 

Who is offering to buy my HTE shares?

Our name is Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc. We
are a Florida corporation and a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard Data Systems Inc. Since our organization, our only activities have been related to making a tender offer for all of the outstanding shares of common stock of HTE. SunGard is a global
leader in integrated information-technology solutions for financial services and is also a leading provider of information availability services. See Introduction and Section 9 (Certain Information Concerning the Purchaser and SunGard) of this Offer
to Purchase for more information about SunGard and us. 

How
many shares of HTE common stock are you offering to purchase? 

We are making an offer to purchase all of the outstanding shares of common stock of HTE. See Introduction and Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

How much are you offering to pay for my shares of HTE common stock, what is
the form of payment and will I have to pay any fees or commissions if I tender my shares in your offer? 

We are offering to pay $7.00 per share in cash (without interest) for each share of your HTE common stock. If you are the record owner of
your shares and you tender them in our offer, you will not have to pay any brokerage fees or similar expenses to do so. If you own your shares through a broker or other nominee, and your broker tenders your shares in our offer on your behalf, your
broker or nominee may charge you a fee for doing so. You should consult your broker or nominee to determine whether it will charge you a fee for tendering your shares in our offer. See Introduction and Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) of this Offer to
Purchase for more information. 

Do you have the financial
resources to pay for all of the shares of HTE common stock that you are offering to purchase? 

Yes. Our parent company, SunGard Data Systems Inc., will contribute or loan to us sufficient funds to pay for all of the shares of HTE
common stock that are accepted for payment by us in the offer and to make any payments for all of the shares of HTE common stock that are not purchased in our offer and that will be converted into the right to receive $7.00 per share in cash in the
merger described below, following the successful completion of our offer. SunGard expects to use its existing cash resources or funds borrowed under its existing line of credit, or a combination of both, to make these contributions or loans. Our
offer is not conditioned upon any financing arrangements or financing contingencies. See Section 10 (Source and Amount of Funds) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 



Is your financial condition
relevant to my decision whether to tender my shares of HTE common stock in your offer? 

No. We do not believe that our financial condition is relevant to your decision whether to tender your shares of HTE common stock in our offer because: 



cash is the only consideration that we are paying to the holders of HTE common stock in connection with our offer; 



we are offering to purchase all of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock in our offer; 



our offer is not subject to any financing arrangements or financing contingencies; and 



SunGard has sufficient cash on hand and cash equivalents, or has sufficient availability under its existing line of credit, to provide us with the amount of cash
consideration payable to holders of HTE common stock in our offer and the merger described below. 

See Section 10 (Source and Amount of Funds) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

How long do I have to tender my shares of HTE common stock in your offer?

Unless we extend our offer, you will have
until 12:00 midnight, New York City time, on Friday, March 14, 2003, to tender your shares of HTE common stock in our offer. If you cannot deliver everything that is required to tender your shares by that time, you may be able to use a guaranteed
delivery procedure to tender your shares, as described in Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) and Section 2 (Procedures for Tendering Shares of HTE Common Stock in the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase. 

Under what circumstances can or must you extend your offer?

We are permitted to (but not required to)
extend our offer beyond its initial expiration date of Friday, March 14, 2003: 



for any period required by any rule, regulation, interpretation or position of the Securities and Exchange Commission applicable to our offer;



for such amount of time as is reasonably necessary to cause all of the conditions to our offer to be satisfied; and 



for an additional period or periods of not more than 20 business days in the aggregate, if the sum of the number of shares of HTE common stock that have been
validly tendered and not withdrawn in our offer as of the scheduled or any extended expiration date of our offer, plus the number of shares of HTE common stock then solely beneficially owned by SunGard and us as of such date, represents a majority
of HTE adjusted outstanding shares (as described below) but less than 80% of HTEs adjusted outstanding shares as of such date. 

In addition, if any of the conditions to our offer have not been satisfied by 12:00 midnight, New York City
time, on Friday, March 14, 2003, the initial expiration date of our offer (or by any additional expiration date if the Offer is extended), we will extend our offer by 10 business days, if so requested by HTE in writing, but we are not required to
extend our offer more than one time at HTEs request. See Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

At our option, we may (but are not required to) also provide for a subsequent offering period, and one or more extensions thereof,
following the expiration of and acceptance of shares tendered in our offer. During any subsequent offering period, if there is one, you could tender your shares to us for the same offer price payable in our offer. See Section 1 (Terms of the Offer)
of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 



How will I be notified if
you extend your offer? 

If we extend our
offer, we will inform the Depositary of that fact and will make a public announcement of the extension, not later than 9:00 a.m., New York City time, on the next business day after the day on which our offer was previously scheduled to expire. See
Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

What are the most significant conditions to your offer? 

We are not obligated to purchase any shares of HTE common stock that are tendered in our offer unless, prior to the expiration of our offer (as it may be extended), the number of shares validly
tendered in accordance with the terms of our offer and not properly withdrawn, together with the shares of HTE common stock then solely beneficially owned by SunGard and us, represents a majority of the number of shares constituting the sum of all
then outstanding shares of HTE common stock plus all shares of HTE common stock issuable upon the exercise of all then outstanding options (which number of shares we refer to in this Summary Term Sheet as the adjusted outstanding shares
of HTE, and which condition we refer to as the minimum condition in this Summary Term Sheet). 

Our offer is not subject to any financing arrangements or financing contingencies, but it is subject to a number of other conditions,
including with respect to the accuracy of HTEs representations and warranties in the merger agreement, HTEs compliance with its covenants set forth in the merger agreement, the absence of a material adverse effect on HTE and its
subsidiaries, and compliance with applicable antitrust law and regulations including the Hart-Scott-Rodino Antitrust Improvement Act of 1976, as amended. See Section 13 (Certain Conditions to the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase for more information
about these and other conditions to our offer. 

Without HTEs consent, we can waive any condition to our offer, other than the minimum condition. 

How do I tender my shares of HTE common stock in your offer? 

To tender all or any portion of your shares of HTE common stock in our offer, you must either deliver the
certificate or certificates representing your tendered shares, with the Letter of Transmittal (or a facsimile copy of it) enclosed with this Offer to Purchase, properly completed and duly executed, together with any required signature guarantees,
and any other required documents, to the Depositary, Wells Fargo Bank Minnesota, N.A., or tender your shares using the book-entry procedure described in Section 2 (Procedures for Tendering Shares of HTE Common Stock in the Offer), prior to the
expiration of our offer. 

If you hold your shares
of HTE common stock in street name through a broker, dealer, bank, trust company or other nominee and you wish to tender all or any portion of your shares of HTE common stock in our offer, the broker, dealer, bank, trust company or other nominee
that holds your shares must tender them on your behalf through the Depositary. 

If you cannot deliver the items that are required to be delivered to the Depositary by the expiration of our offer, you may obtain additional time to do so by having a broker, bank or other fiduciary
that is a member of the Securities Transfer Agents Medallion Program or other eligible institution guarantee that the missing items will be received by the Depositary within three Nasdaq Stock Market trading days. You may use the Notice of
Guaranteed Delivery enclosed with this Offer to Purchase for this purpose. To tender shares of HTE common stock in this manner, however, the Depositary must receive the required items within such three trading day period. See Section 2 (Procedures
for Tendering Shares of HTE Common Stock in the Offer) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 



Can I withdraw shares that
I previously tendered in your offer? Until what time may I withdraw previously tendered shares? 

Yes. You can withdraw some or all of the shares of HTE common stock that you previously tendered in our offer at any time until the
expiration date of our offer as it may be extended. Further, if we have not accepted your shares for payment by April 15, 2003, you can withdraw them at any time after April 15, 2003. Once we accept your tendered shares for payment upon the
expiration of our offer, however, you will no longer be able to withdraw them. In addition, your right to withdraw your previously tendered shares will not apply to any subsequent offering period (which is not the same as an extension of our offer),
if one is provided. See Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) and Section 3 (Withdrawal Rights) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

How do I withdraw my previously tendered shares? 

To withdraw any shares of HTE common stock that you previously tendered in our offer, you (or, if your shares are held in street name, the
broker, dealer, bank, trust company or other nominee that holds your shares) must deliver a written notice of withdrawal (or a facsimile copy of one), with the required information, to the Depositary while you still have the right to withdraw your
shares. See Section 1 (Terms of the Offer) and Section 3 (Withdrawal Rights) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

Has HTEs board of directors approved your offer? 

Yes. Our offer is being made pursuant to an Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated February 4, 2003, by and among SunGard, HTE and us.
HTEs board of directors has, by the unanimous vote of all directors of HTE: 



determined that the merger agreement and the transactions contemplated by the merger agreement, including our offer and the merger, are fair to and in the best
interests of HTE shareholders; 



adopted and approved the merger agreement and approved the transactions contemplated by the merger agreement, including our offer and the merger;



declared that the merger agreement is advisable; and 



resolved to recommend that the shareholders of HTE accept the Offer and tender their shares of HTE common stock in the Offer. 

Accordingly, HTEs board of directors unanimously
recommends that you accept our offer and tender your shares of HTE common stock pursuant to our offer and, if required, vote to adopt the merger agreement. 

The factors considered by HTEs board of directors in making the determinations and the recommendation described above are described
in HTEs Solicitation/Recommendation Statement on Schedule 14D-9, which has been filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission and is being mailed to the shareholders of HTE with this Offer to Purchase. Shareholders of HTE are urged to
carefully read HTEs Solicitation/Recommendation Statement on Schedule 14D-9 in its entirety. 

Broadview International LLC delivered an opinion to HTEs board of directors, dated February 3, 2003, to the effect that, as of such
date and subject to the assumptions and limitations stated in its written opinion, the offer price to be paid to shareholders whose shares of HTE common stock are accepted for payment in our offer and to be paid to shareholders in the merger was
fair, from a financial point of view, to the holders of shares of HTE common stock. The opinion of Broadview International LLC is addressed only to the HTE board of directors. It relates only to the fairness, from a financial point of view, of the
$7.00 in cash per share to be received by shareholders whose shares are accepted for payment in the Offer, and it does not constitute a recommendation to any shareholder as to whether or not a shareholder should tender shares in our offer or as to
how a shareholder should vote at a shareholders meeting, if any, held in connection with a merger involving SunGard and/or the Purchaser and HTE. HTE shareholders are urged to read the opinion in its entirety. 



SunGard has
retained Broadview International LLC in connection with certain other acquisitions made by SunGard; however, Broadview International LLC was not engaged by, and did not represent, SunGard or the Purchaser with respect to the negotiations concerning
HTE or the fairness opinion issued to HTEs board of directors. See Introduction of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

Have any shareholders of HTE already agreed to tender their shares in your offer? 

Yes. Each of HTEs directors, Tyler Technologies, Inc. and Constellation Software, Inc. have entered
into tender and voting agreements with SunGard and us pursuant to which they have agreed, in their capacity as shareholders of HTE, to tender all of their respective shares of HTE common stock, and, in the case of Tyler Technologies, Inc. and
Constellation Software, Inc., any additional shares of HTE common stock that they may acquire, in our offer. As of February 3, 2003, such directors and shareholders held in the aggregate 7,884,402 shares of HTE common stock, which represented
approximately 43.2% of all then outstanding shares of HTE common stock, including shares issuable upon exercise of HTE stock options and pursuant to HTEs 1997 Employee Stock Purchase Plan. 

What are your plans if you successfully complete your offer but do not
acquire all of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock in your offer? 

If we successfully complete our offer and certain limited conditions are satisfied, as soon as practicable following the successful completion of our offer, we intend to merge with and into HTE. As a
result of that merger, (i) all of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock that are not tendered in our offer, other than shares that are owned by SunGard, HTE or us or any wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard or HTE, will be canceled and converted
into the right to receive $7.00 in cash, (ii) any shares of HTE common stock owned by SunGard, HTE or us will be canceled without consideration and (iii) each of our issued and outstanding shares of capital stock that are owned by SunGard will be
converted into one share of HTE common stock, as a result of which SunGard will own all of the issued and outstanding shares of HTE. 

Our obligation to merge with HTE following the successful completion of our offer is conditioned on the requisite adoption of the merger
agreement by HTEs shareholders under Florida law having been obtained and no temporary restraining order, preliminary or permanent injunction or other order preventing the completion of the merger having been issued by any court of competent
jurisdiction and remaining in effect, and there not being any law enacted or deemed applicable to the merger that makes completion of the merger illegal. If we successfully complete our offer, we will hold a sufficient number of shares of HTE common
stock to ensure that we will obtain the requisite adoption of the merger agreement by HTE shareholders under Florida law to complete the merger. In addition, if we own at least 80% of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock after purchasing
shares in our offer, we will not be required to obtain shareholder approval to complete the merger. 

If you successfully complete your offer, what will happen to HTEs board of directors? 

If we successfully complete our offer, under the merger agreement we are entitled to designate a number of individuals who will become
directors of HTE. The number of directors that we will be entitled to designate generally will comprise the same percentage of the total board of directors as the number of shares of HTE common stock we purchase in the offer comprises of HTEs
total outstanding shares. For example, if 75% of HTEs total outstanding shares are validly tendered and not withdrawn and are accepted by us for payment in our offer, we will be entitled to designate approximately 75% of the members of
HTEs board of directors. HTE has agreed to take all reasonable action necessary to ensure that our designees are elected or appointed to its board of directors. Therefore, if we successfully complete our offer, we will obtain control over the
management of HTE shortly thereafter. However, we have agreed in the merger agreement that we and HTE will use commercially reasonable efforts to ensure that at least two of the members of HTEs board of directors, at all times prior to the
completion of the merger, are individuals who were directors of HTE and were not officers or employees of HTE or any of its subsidiaries on February 4, 2003, the date of the merger agreement. After the election or appointment of the directors
designated by us to HTEs board of directors and prior to the completion of the 



merger, under the terms of the merger agreement, the approval of the individuals who were directors of HTE and were not officers or employees
of HTE or any of its subsidiaries on February 4, 2003 (which directors we refer to below as continuing HTE directors) will be required to (i) amend or terminate the merger agreement on behalf of HTE, (ii) extend the time for performance
of, or waive compliance with, any of the agreements or conditions contained in the merger agreement for the benefit of HTE, (iii) authorize any required or permitted consent or action by HTEs board of directors under the merger agreement or
(iv) authorize any other action of HTE under the merger agreement which adversely affects the holders of shares of HTE common stock (other than SunGard or us), provided, that if for any reason there are no continuing HTE directors and
HTE has used commercially reasonable efforts to appoint continuing HTE directors, such actions may be effected by majority vote of HTEs entire board of directors. See Section 12 (Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE; The Merger
Agreement; The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

If I decide not to tender my shares of HTE common stock in your offer, how will your offer affect my shares? 

If we successfully complete our offer, but you do not tender your shares in our offer, and the merger takes
place, your shares will be canceled and converted into the right to receive the same amount of cash that you would have received had you tendered your shares in our offer. Therefore, if we complete the merger, the only difference to you between
having your shares accepted for payment in our offer and not doing so is that you will be paid earlier if you have your shares accepted for payment. 

Until such time, if ever, as we complete the merger, the number of shareholders of HTE and the number of shares of HTE common stock that
remain in the hands of the public may be so small that there may no longer be an active public trading market (or, possibly, any public trading market) for such shares. Also, shares of HTE common stock may no longer be eligible to be traded on the
Nasdaq National Market or any other securities exchange, and HTE may cease making filings with the Securities and Exchange Commission or otherwise cease being required to comply with the Securities and Exchange Commissions rules relating to
publicly held companies. See Section 7 (Effect of the Offer on the Market for Shares of HTE Common Stock; Nasdaq Listing of Shares of HTE Common Stock; Exchange Act Registration of Shares of HTE Common Stock; Margin Regulations) and Section 12
(Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE; The Merger Agreement; The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

Are dissenters rights available in either your offer or the merger? 

Dissenters or appraisal rights are not available in connection with our offer or the merger. See
Section 12 (Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE; The Merger Agreement; The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

What are the United States federal income tax consequences of having my shares of HTE common stock accepted for payment in your offer?

The receipt of cash pursuant to our offer
(or the merger) will be a taxable transaction for United States federal income tax purposes under the Internal Revenue Code of 1986, as amended, and may also be a taxable transaction under applicable state, local or foreign income or other tax laws.
Generally, for United States federal income tax purposes, a shareholder having his shares of HTE common stock accepted for payment in our offer or receiving cash in the merger will recognize gain or loss equal to the difference between the amount of
cash received by the shareholder in our offer (or the merger) and the shareholders aggregate adjusted tax basis in the shares tendered by the shareholder and accepted for payment in our offer (or converted into cash in the merger). Gain or
loss will be calculated separately for each block of shares tendered and accepted for payment in the offer (or converted into cash in the merger). See Section 5 (Certain United States Federal Income Tax Consequences) of this Offer to Purchase for
more information. 



Shareholders are urged to consult their own tax advisors to determine the particular tax consequences to them (including the application and effect of any state, local or foreign income and other tax laws) of our offer and the
merger. 

What is the market value of my shares of HTE
common stock? 

On February 4, 2003, the last
trading day before SunGard and HTE announced that they had entered into the merger agreement, the last sale price of shares of HTE common stock reported on the Nasdaq National Market was $4.74 per share; therefore, the offer price of $7.00 per share
represents a premium of 47.7% over the closing price of the HTE shares before announcement of the merger agreement. On February 13, 2003, the last full trading day prior to the commencement of our offer, the last sale price of shares of HTE common
stock reported on the Nasdaq National Market was $6.922 per share. We advise you to obtain a recent quotation for shares of HTE common stock when deciding whether to tender your shares in our offer. See Section 6 (Price Range of Shares of HTE Common
Stock; Dividends on Shares of HTE Common Stock) of this Offer to Purchase for more information.

INTRODUCTION 

Lake Acquisition Corp. Inc., a Florida corporation (the
Purchaser) and a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard Data Systems Inc., a Delaware corporation (SunGard), hereby offers to purchase all of the outstanding shares of common stock, par value $0.01 per share, of H.T.E., Inc., a
Florida corporation (HTE), at a price of $7.00 per share, in cash, without interest thereon (the Offer Price), upon the terms and subject to the conditions set forth in this Offer to Purchase and the related Letter of
Transmittal enclosed with this Offer to Purchase, which, together with any amendments or supplements hereto or thereto, collectively constitute the Offer described in this Offer to Purchase. 

Tendering HTE shareholders whose shares of HTE common stock
are registered in their own names and who tender their shares directly to Wells Fargo Bank Minnesota, N.A., which is acting as the Depositary for the Offer, will not be obligated to pay brokerage fees or commissions in connection with the Offer or,
except as set forth in Instruction 6 of the Letter of Transmittal for the Offer, transfer taxes on the sale of shares in the Offer. A shareholder of HTE who holds shares of HTE common stock through a broker, dealer, bank, trust company or other
nominee should consult with such institution to determine whether it will charge any service fees for tendering such shareholders shares to the Purchaser in the Offer. 

The Purchaser will pay all fees and expenses of the Depositary and D.F. King & Co., Inc., the information
agent for the Offer (the Information Agent), incurred in connection with the Offer. See Section 15 (Fees and Expenses) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

The Offer is being made pursuant to an Agreement and Plan of Merger, dated February 4, 2003, by and among
SunGard, the Purchaser and HTE (the Merger Agreement) pursuant to which, following the purchase by the Purchaser of shares of HTE common stock in the Offer and the satisfaction or waiver of certain conditions, the Purchaser will be
merged with and into HTE (the Merger), with HTE surviving the Merger as a wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard. As a result of the Merger, (i) each outstanding share of HTE common stock (other than shares owned by SunGard, the Purchaser,
HTE or any wholly owned subsidiary of SunGard or HTE) will be converted into the right to receive the Offer Price, without interest thereon, (ii) any shares of HTE common stock owned by SunGard, the Purchaser or HTE will be canceled without
consideration and (iii) each issued and outstanding share of capital stock of the Purchaser that are owned by SunGard will be converted into one share of HTE common stock, as a result of which SunGard will own all of the issued and outstanding
shares of HTE. See Section 12 (Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE; The Merger Agreement; The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

HTEs board of directors has, at a meeting held on February 1, 2003, by the unanimous vote of all
directors of HTE, (i) determined that the Merger Agreement and the transactions contemplated thereby, including the Offer and the Merger, are fair to, and in the best interests of, the shareholders of HTE; (ii) adopted and approved the Merger
Agreement and approved the transactions contemplated thereby, including the Offer and the Merger; (iii) declared that the Merger Agreement is advisable; and (iv) resolved to recommend that the shareholders of HTE accept the Offer and tender their
shares in the Offer. Accordingly, HTEs board of directors unanimously recommends that the shareholders of HTE accept the Offer and tender their shares of HTE common stock to the Purchaser in the Offer and, if required, vote to adopt the Merger
Agreement. 



The factors
considered by HTEs board of directors in making the determinations and the recommendation described above are described in HTEs Solicitation/Recommendation Statement on Schedule 14D-9 (the Schedule 14D-9), which has been
filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission and is being mailed to the shareholders of HTE with this Offer to Purchase. Shareholders of HTE are urged to carefully read HTEs Solicitation/Recommendation Statement on Schedule 14D-9 in its
entirety.

holders of shares of HTE common stock. The opinion of Broadview International LLC is addressed only to the HTE board of directors. It relates only to the fairness, from a financial point of view, of the $7.00 in cash per share to be received by
shareholders whose shares are accepted for payment in the Offer, and it does not constitute a recommendation to any shareholder as to whether or not a shareholder should tender shares in the Offer or as to how a shareholder should vote at a
shareholders meeting, if any, held in connection with the Merger. HTE shareholders are urged to read the opinion in its entirety. 

SunGard has previously retained Broadview International LLC in connection with certain other acquisitions made by SunGard; however,
Broadview International LLC was not engaged by, and did not represent, SunGard or the Purchaser with respect to the negotiations concerning HTE or the fairness opinion issued to HTEs board of directors. During 2002, SunGard paid to Broadview
International LLC an annual retainer of $30,000 and approximately $5,000 in reimbursable expenses. During 2001, SunGard paid to Broadview an annual retainer of $30,000, fees of $4,125,000 in connection with SunGards November 2001 acquisition
of the availability solutions business of Comdisco, Inc., and approximately $5,000 in reimbursable expenses. During 2000, SunGard paid approximately $44,100 to Broadview in connection with an annual retainer and reimbursable expenses. In addition, a
director of SunGard, Bernard Goldstein, was a director of Broadview until his retirement in December 2002. Mr. Goldstein abstained from voting on the proposed transaction in his capacity as a director of SunGard. 

The Offer is conditioned upon, among other things, there being
validly tendered in accordance with the terms of the Offer and not properly withdrawn prior to the Expiration Date (as defined in Section 1 of this Offer to Purchase) of the Offer (excluding shares tendered by notice of guaranteed delivery that have
not been delivered to the Depositary by the Expiration Date) that number of shares of HTE common stock that, together with the shares of HTE common stock then solely beneficially owned by the Purchaser and SunGard (if any), represent a majority of
the number of shares constituting the sum of all then outstanding shares of HTE common stock, plus all shares of HTE common stock issuable upon the exercise of all then outstanding options (which number of shares is referred to herein as HTEs
Adjusted Outstanding Shares and which condition is referred to herein as the Minimum Condition). The Offer is also subject to other conditions described in Section 13 (Certain Conditions to the Offer) of this Offer to
Purchase. 

Each of HTEs directors, Tyler
Technologies, Inc. and Constellation Software, Inc. have entered into tender and voting agreements with SunGard and the Purchaser (the Tender and Voting Agreements) pursuant to which they have agreed, in their capacity as shareholders of
HTE, to tender all of their shares of HTE common stock and, in the case of Tyler Technologies, Inc. and Constellation Software, Inc., any additional shares of HTE common stock that they may acquire, to the Purchaser in the Offer. As of February 3,
2003, such directors and shareholders held in the aggregate 7,884,402 shares of HTE common stock, which represented approximately 43.2% of HTEs Adjusted Outstanding Shares as of such date. See Section 12 (Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE;
The Merger Agreement; The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase. 



Completion of
the Merger is subject to the satisfaction of a number of conditions, including (i) the purchase of shares of HTE common stock by the Purchaser in the Offer and (ii) the adoption of the Merger Agreement by the affirmative vote of the holders of a
majority of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock, if required by applicable law. If the Offer is successfully completed, the Purchaser will have sufficient voting power to adopt the Merger Agreement without the affirmative vote of any other
holder of HTE common stock. In addition, if the Purchaser owns 80% or more of the outstanding shares of HTE common stock after purchasing shares in the Offer, under applicable law, the Purchaser and SunGard will be able to complete the Merger
without obtaining the adoption of the Merger Agreement by the remaining holders of HTE common stock who have not tendered their shares of HTE common stock in the Offer. In such event, under the terms of the Merger Agreement, SunGard, the Purchaser
and HTE have agreed to take all necessary and appropriate action to cause the Merger to become effective as soon as practicable after the successful completion of the Offer. See Section 12 (Purpose of the Offer; Plans for HTE; The Merger Agreement;
The Tender and Voting Agreements) of this Offer to Purchase for more information. 

HTE has informed the Purchaser that, as of February 3, 2003, there were: (i) 15,901,523 shares of HTE common stock issued and outstanding; (ii) 2,331,921 shares of HTE common stock subject to
outstanding options; and (iii) up to 5,951 shares to be issued by HTE pursuant to HTEs 1997 Employee Stock Purchase Plan. Based upon the foregoing, the Minimum Condition will be satisfied if at least approximately 9,119,699 shares of HTE
common stock are validly tendered (including shares tendered pursuant to the Tender and Voting Agreements) and not withdrawn prior to the Expiration Date of the Offer. Assuming that all 7,884,402 shares subject to the Tender and Voting Agreements
are validly tendered and not withdrawn prior to the Expiration Date of the Offer, approximately 1,235,297 shares of HTE common stock (approximately 6.8% of HTEs Adjusted Outstanding Shares) must be validly tendered and not withdrawn prior to
the Expiration Date of the Offer to satisfy the Minimum Condition. The actual number of shares of HTE common stock that are required to be tendered to satisfy the Minimum Condition will depend upon the actual number of Adjusted Outstanding Shares
prior to the Expiration Date. 

Certain U.S.
federal income tax consequences of the sale of shares of HTE common stock in the Offer and the conversion of shares of HTE common stock into cash pursuant to the Merger are described in Section 5 (Certain United States Federal Income Tax
Consequences) of this Offer to Purchase.

between the date of the Merger Agreement and the date on which any particular share of HTE common stock is accepted for payment in the Offer, the outstanding shares of HTE common stock are changed into a different number or class of shares by reason
of any stock split, division or subdivision of shares, stock dividend, reverse stock split, consolidation of shares, reclassification, recapitalization or other similar transaction, then the Offer Price will be appropriately adjusted to reflect such
change or transaction.
